defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\\n86: /*\\n87:  * Helper read-from-socket functions. Does the same as Curl_read() but it\\n88:  * blocks until all bytes amount of buffersize will be read. No more, no less.\\n89:  *\\n90:  * This is STUPID BLOCKING behavior. Only used by the SOCKS GSSAPI functions.\\n91:  */\\n92: int Curl_blockread_all(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n93:                        struct Curl_easy *data,   /* transfer */\\n94:                        char *buf,                /* store read data here */\\n95:                        ssize_t buffersize,       /* max amount to read */\\n96:                        ssize_t *n)               /* amount bytes read */\\n97: {\\n98:   ssize_t nread = 0;\\n99:   ssize_t allread = 0;\\n100:   int result;\\n101:   CURLcode err = CURLE_OK;\\n102: \\n103:   *n = 0;\\n104:   for(;;) {\\n105:     timediff_t change state, to make debugging easier */\\n154: static void socksstate(struct socks_state *sx, struct Curl_easy *data,\\n155:                        enum connect_t state\\n156: #ifdef \\n232: static CURLproxycode socks_state_recv(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n233:                                       struct socks_state *sx,\\n234:                                       struct Curl_easy *data,\\n235:                                       CURLproxycode failcode,\\n236:                                       const char *description)\\n237: {\\n238:   ssize_t nread;\\n239:   CURLcode result;\\n240: \\n241:   nread = Curl_conn_cf_recv(cf->next, data, (char *)sx->outp,\\n242:                             sx->outstanding, &result);\\n243:   if(nread <= 0) {\\n244: CURLPX_OK;\\n261: }\\n262: \\n263: /*\\n264: * This function logs in to a SOCKS4 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\\n265: * destination server.\\n266: *\\n267: * Reference :\\n268: *   https://www.openssh.com/txt/socks4.protocol\\n269: *\\n270: * Note :\\n271: *   Set protocol4a=true for  \\\"SOCKS 4A (Simple Extension to SOCKS 4 Protocol)\\\"\\n272: *   Nonsupport \\\"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\\\"\\n273: */\\n274: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS4(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n275:                                struct socks_state *sx,\\n276:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\\n277: {\\n278:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\\n279:   const bool protocol4a =\\n280:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS4A) ? TRUE : FALSE;\\n281:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\\n282:   CURLcode result;\\n283:   CURLproxycode presult;\\n284:   struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\\n285: \\n286:   /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\\n287:   DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\\n288: \\n289:   switch(sx->state) {\\n290:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\\n291:     /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\\n292:     conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\\n293:     if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\\n294:       infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\\\",\\n295:             protocol4a ? \\\"a\\\" : \\\"\\\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\\n296: \\n297:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\\\",\\n298:           sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\\n299: \\n300:     /*\\n301:      * Compose socks4 request\\n302:      *\\n303:      * Request format\\n304:      *\\n305:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\\n306:      *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\\n307:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\\n308:      * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\\n309:      */\\n310: \\n311:     socksreq[0] = 4; /* version (SOCKS4) */\\n312:     socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\\n313:     socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\\n314:     socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff);        /* LSB */\\n315: \\n316:     /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\\n317:     if(!protocol4a) {\\n318:       enum resolve_t rc =\\n319:         Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\\n320: \\n321:       if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\\n322:         return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n323:       else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\\n324:         sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\\n325:         infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\\\", sx->hostname);\\n326:         return CURLPX_OK;\\n327:       }\\n328:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\\n329:       goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\\n330:     }\\n331: \\n332:     /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\\n333:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\\n334:     goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\\n335: \\n336:   case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\\n337:     /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\\n338:     dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\\n339: \\n340:     if(dns) {\\n341: #ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\\n342:       data->state.async.dns = dns;\\n343:       data->state.async.done = TRUE;\\n344: #endif\\n345:       infof(data, \\\"Hostname '%s' was found\\\", sx->hostname);\\n346:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\\n347:     }\\n348:     else {\\n349:       result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\\n350:       if(!dns) {\\n351:         if(result)\\n352:           return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n353:         return CURLPX_OK;\\n354:       }\\n355:     }\\n356:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n357: CONNECT_RESOLVED:\\n358:   case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\\n359:     struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\\n360:     /*\\n361:      * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\\n362:      * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\\n363:      */\\n364:     if(dns) {\\n365:       hp = dns->addr;\\n366: \\n367:       /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\\n368:       while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\\n369:         hp = hp->ai_next;\\n370: \\n371:       if(hp) {\\n372:         struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\\n373:         char buf[64];\\n374:         Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\\n375: \\n376:         saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\\n377:         socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\\n378:         socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\\n379:         socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\\n380:         socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\\n381: \\n382:         infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\\\", buf);\\n383: \\n384:         Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\\n385:       }\\n386:       else\\n387:         failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\\\", sx->hostname);\\n388:     }\\n389:     else\\n390:       failf(data, \\\"Failed to resolve \\\\\\\"%s\\\\\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\\\",\\n391:             sx->hostname);\\n392: \\n393:     if(!hp)\\n394:       return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n395:   }\\n396:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n397: CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n398:   case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n399:     /*\\n400:      * This is currently not supporting \\\"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\\\".\\n401:      */\\n402:     socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\\n406:         failf(data, \\\"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\\\");\\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\\n408:       }\\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\\n411:     }\\n412: \\n413:     /*\\n414:      * Make connection\\n415:      */\\n416:     {\\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\\n419: \\n420:       /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\\n421:       if(protocol4a) {\\n422:         size_t hostnamelen = 0;\\n423:         socksreq[4] = 0;\\n424:         socksreq[5] = 0;\\n425:         socksreq[6] = 0;\\n426:         socksreq[7] = 1;\\n427:         /* append hostname */\\n428:         hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\\n429:         if(hostnamelen <= 255)\\n430:           strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\\n431:         else {\\n432:           failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4: too long host name\\\");\\n433:           return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\\n434:         }\\n435:         packetsize += hostnamelen;\\n436:       }\\n437:       sx->outp = socksreq;\\n438:       sx->outstanding = packetsize;\\n439:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\\n440:     }\\n441:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n442:   case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\\n443:     /* Send request */\\n444:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\\n445:                                \\\"SOCKS4 connect request\\\");\\n446:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n447:       return presult;\\n448:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n449:       /* remain in sending state */\\n450:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n451:     }\\n452:     /* done sending! */\\n453:     sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\\n454:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n455:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\\n456: \\n457:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n458:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\\n459:     /* Receive response */\\n460:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\\n461:                                \\\"connect request ack\\\");\\n462:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n463:       return presult;\\n464:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n465:       /* remain in reading state */\\n466:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n467:     }\\n468:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\\n469:     break;\\n470:   default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\\n471:     break;\\n472:   }\\n473: \\n474:   /*\\n475:    * Response format\\n476:    *\\n477:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\\n478:    *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\\n479:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\\n480:    * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\\n481:    *\\n482:    * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. CD is the result\\n483:    * code with one of the following values:\\n484:    *\\n485:    * 90: request granted\\n486:    * 91: request rejected or failed\\n487:    * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\\n488:    *     identd on the client\\n489:    * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\\n490:    *     report different user-ids\\n491:    */\\n492: \\n493:   /* wrong version ? */\\n494:   if(socksreq[0]) {\\n495:     failf(data,\\n496:           \\\"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\\\");\\n497:     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n498:   }\\n499: \\n500:   /* Result */\\n501:   switch(socksreq[1]) {\\n502:   case 90:\\n503:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s request granted.\\\", protocol4a?\\\"a\\\":\\\"\\\");\\n504:     break;\\n505:   case 91:\\n506:     failf(data,\\n507:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n508:           \\\", request rejected or failed.\\\",\\n509:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n510:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n511:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n512:     return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\\n513:   case 92:\\n514:     failf(data,\\n515:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n516:           \\\", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \\\"\\n517:           \\\"identd on the client.\\\",\\n518:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n519:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n520:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n521:     return CURLPX_IDENTD;\\n522:   case 93:\\n523:     failf(data,\\n524:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n525:           \\\", request rejected because the client program and identd \\\"\\n526:           \\\"report different user-ids.\\\",\\n527:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n528:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n529:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n530:     return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\\n531:   default:\\n532:     failf(data,\\n533:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n534:           \\\", Unknown.\\\",\\n535:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n536:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n537:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n538:     return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\\n539:   }\\n540: \\n541:   return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\\n542: }\\n543: \\n544: /*\\n545:  * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\\n546:  * destination server.\\n547:  */\\n548: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n549:                                struct socks_state *sx,\\n550:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\\n551: {\\n552:   /*\\n553:     According to the RFC1928, section \\\"6.  Replies\\\". This is what a SOCK5\\n554:     replies:\\n555: \\n556:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n557:         |VER | REP |  RSV  | ATYP | BND.ADDR | BND.PORT |\\n558:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n559:         | 1  |  1  | X'00' |  1   | Variable |    2     |\\n560:         +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\\n561: \\n562:     Where:\\n563: \\n564:     o  VER    protocol version: X'05'\\n565:     o  REP    Reply field:\\n566:     o  X'00' succeeded\\n567:   */\\n568:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\\n569:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\\n570:   int idx;\\n571:   CURLcode result;\\n572:   CURLproxycode presult;\\n573:   bool socks5_resolve_local =\\n574:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5) ? /* not used anymore from now on */\\n385:       }\\n386:       else\\n387:         failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\\\", sx->hostname);\\n388:     }\\n389:     else\\n390:       failf(data, \\\"Failed to resolve \\\\\\\"%s\\\\\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\\\",\\n391:             sx->hostname);\\n392: \\n393:     if(!hp)\\n394:       return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\\n395:   }\\n396:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n397: CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n398:   case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\\n399:     /*\\n400:      * This is currently not supporting \\\"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\\\".\\n401:      */\\n402:     socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\\n406:         failf(data, \\\"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\\\");\\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\\n408:       }\\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\\n411:     }\\n412: \\n413:     /*\\n414:      * Make connection\\n415:      */\\n416:     {\\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\\n419: \\n420:       /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\\n421:       if(protocol4a) {\\n422:         size_t hostnamelen = 0;\\n423:         socksreq[4] = 0;\\n424:         socksreq[5] = 0;\\n425:         socksreq[6] = 0;\\n426:         socksreq[7] = 1;\\n427:         /* append hostname */\\n428:         hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\\n429:         if(hostnamelen <= 255)\\n430:           strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\\n431:         else {\\n432:           failf(data, \\\"SOCKS4: too long host name\\\");\\n433:           return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\\n434:         }\\n435:         packetsize += hostnamelen;\\n436:       }\\n437:       sx->outp = socksreq;\\n438:       sx->outstanding = packetsize;\\n439:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\\n440:     }\\n441:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n442:   case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\\n443:     /* Send request */\\n444:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\\n445:                                \\\"SOCKS4 connect request\\\");\\n446:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n447:       return presult;\\n448:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n449:       /* remain in sending state */\\n450:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n451:     }\\n452:     /* done sending! */\\n453:     sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\\n454:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n455:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\\n456: \\n457:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n458:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\\n459:     /* Receive response */\\n460:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\\n461:                                \\\"connect request ack\\\");\\n462:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n463:       return presult;\\n464:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n465:       /* remain in reading state */\\n466:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n467:     }\\n468:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\\n469:     break;\\n470:   default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\\n471:     break;\\n472:   }\\n473: \\n474:   /*\\n475:    * Response format\\n476:    *\\n477:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\\n478:    *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\\n479:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\\n480:    * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\\n481:    *\\n482:    * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. CD is the result\\n483:    * code with one of the following values:\\n484:    *\\n485:    * 90: request granted\\n486:    * 91: request rejected or failed\\n487:    * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\\n488:    *     identd on the client\\n489:    * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\\n490:    *     report different user-ids\\n491:    */\\n492: \\n493:   /* wrong version ? */\\n494:   if(socksreq[0]) {\\n495:     failf(data,\\n496:           \\\"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\\\");\\n497:     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n498:   }\\n499: \\n500:   /* Result */\\n501:   switch(socksreq[1]) {\\n502:   case 90:\\n503:     infof(data, \\\"SOCKS4%s request granted.\\\", protocol4a?\\\"a\\\":\\\"\\\");\\n504:     break;\\n505:   case 91:\\n506:     failf(data,\\n507:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n508:           \\\", request rejected or failed.\\\",\\n509:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n510:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n511:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n512:     return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\\n513:   case 92:\\n514:     failf(data,\\n515:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n516:           \\\", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \\\"\\n517:           \\\"identd on the client.\\\",\\n518:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n519:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n520:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n521:     return CURLPX_IDENTD;\\n522:   case 93:\\n523:     failf(data,\\n524:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n525:           \\\", request rejected because the client program and identd \\\"\\n526:           \\\"report different user-ids.\\\",\\n527:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n528:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n529:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n530:     return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\\n531:   default:\\n532:     failf(data,\\n533:           \\\"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\\\"\\n534:           \\\", Unknown.\\\",\\n535:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\\n536:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\\n537:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\\n538:     return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\\n539:   }\\n540: \\n541:   return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\\n542: }\\n543: \\n544: /*\\n545:  * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\\n546:  * destination server.\\n547:  */\\n548: static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\\n549:                                struct socks_state *sx,\\n550:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\\n551: {\\n552:   /*\\n553:     According to the RFC1928, section \\\"6.  Replies\\\". /* expect two bytes */\\n643:     sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\\n644:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n645:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\\n646:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\\n647:                                \\\"initial SOCKS5 response\\\");\\n648:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n649:       return presult;\\n650:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\\n651:       /* remain in reading state */\\n652:       return CURLPX_OK;\\n653:     }\\n654:     else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\\n655:       failf(data, \\\"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\\\");\\n656:       return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\\n657:     }\\n658:     else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\\n659:       /* DONE! /* the length must fit in a single byte */\\n737:       if(proxy_password_len > 255) {\\n738:         failf(data, \\\"Excessive password length for proxy auth\\\");\\n739:         return CURLPX_LONG_PASSWD;\\n740:       }\\n741:       memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_password, proxy_password_len);\\n742:     }\\n743:     len += proxy_password_len;\\n744:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_SEND);\\n745:     sx->outstanding = len;\\n746:     sx->outp = socksreq;\\n747:   }\\n748:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\\n749:   case CONNECT_AUTH_SEND:\\n750:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_AUTH,\\n751:                                \\\"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation request\\\");\\n752:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\\n753:       return presult;\\n754:     else *sx,\n276:                                struct Curl_easy *data)\n277: {\n278:   struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n279:   const bool protocol4a =\n280:     (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == TRUE : FALSE;\n281:   unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n282:   CURLcode result;\n283:   CURLproxycode presult;\n284:   struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n285: \n286:   /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\n287:   DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\n288: \n289:   switch(sx->state) {\n290:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n291:     /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\n292:     conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\n293:     if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n294:       infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n295:             protocol4a ? \"a\" : \"\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n296: \n297:     infof(data, \"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\",\n298:           sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n299: \n300:     /*\n301:      * Compose socks4 request\n302:      *\n303:      * Request format\n304:      *\n305:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n306:      *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\n307:      *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n308:      * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\n309:      */\n310: \n311:     socksreq[0] = 4;        /* LSB */\n315: \n316:     /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\n317:     if(!protocol4a) {\n318:       enum resolve_t rc =\n319:         Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\n320: \n321:       if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n322:         return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n323:       else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n324:         sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n325:         infof(data, \"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\", sx->hostname);\n326:         return CURLPX_OK;\n327:       }\n328:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n329:       goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n330:     }\n331: \n332:     /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\n333:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n334:     goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n335: \n336:   case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n337:     /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n338:     dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\n339: \n340:     if(dns) {\n341: #ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n342:       data->state.async.dns = dns;\n343:       data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n344: #endif\n345:       infof(data, \"Hostname '%s' was found\", sx->hostname);\n346:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n347:     }\n348:     else {\n349:       result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\n350:       if(!dns) {\n351:         if(result)\n352:           return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n353:         return CURLPX_OK;\n354:       }\n355:     }\n356:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n357: CONNECT_RESOLVED:\n358:   case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\n359:     struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\n360:     /*\n361:      * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\n362:      * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\n363:      */\n364:     if(dns) {\n365:       hp = dns->addr;\n366: \n367:       /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\n368:       while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\n369:         hp = hp->ai_next;\n370: \n371:       if(hp) {\n372:         struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\n373:         char buf[64];\n374:         Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\n375: \n376:         saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\n377:         socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\n378:         socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\n379:         socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\n380:         socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\n381: \n382:         infof(data, \"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\", buf);\n383: \n384:         Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\n385:       }\n386:       else\n387:         failf(data, \"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\", sx->hostname);\n388:     }\n389:     else\n390:       failf(data, \"Failed to resolve \\\"%s\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\",\n391:             sx->hostname);\n392: \n393:     if(!hp)\n394:       return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n395:   }\n396:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n397: CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n398:   case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n399:     /*\n400:      * This is currently not supporting \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\".\n401:      */\n402:     socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\n403:     if(sx->proxy_user) {\n404:       size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n405:       if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\n406:         failf(data, \"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\");\n407:         return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n408:       }\n409:       /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\n410:       memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\n411:     }\n412: \n413:     /*\n414:      * Make connection\n415:      */\n416:     {\n417:       size_t packetsize = 9 +\n418:         strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\n419: \n420:       /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\n421:       if(protocol4a) {\n422:         size_t hostnamelen = 0;\n423:         socksreq[4] = 0;\n424:         socksreq[5] = 0;\n425:         socksreq[6] = 0;\n426:         socksreq[7] = 1;\n427:         /* append hostname */\n428:         hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\n429:         if(hostnamelen <= 255)\n430:           strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\n431:         else {\n432:           failf(data, \"SOCKS4: too long host name\");\n433:           return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\n434:         }\n435:         packetsize += hostnamelen;\n436:       }\n437:       sx->outp = socksreq;\n438:       sx->outstanding = packetsize;\n439:       sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\n440:     }\n441:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n442:   case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\n443:     /* Send request */\n444:     presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n445:                                \"SOCKS4 connect request\");\n446:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n447:       return presult;\n448:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n449:       /* remain in sending state */\n450:       return CURLPX_OK;\n451:     }\n452:     /* done sending! */\n453:     sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\n454:     sx->outp = socksreq;\n455:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n456: \n457:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n458:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n459:     /* Receive response */\n460:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n461:                                \"connect request ack\");\n462:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n463:       return presult;\n464:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n465:       /* remain in reading state */\n466:       return CURLPX_OK;\n467:     }\n468:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\n469:     break;\n470:   default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\n471:     break;\n472:   }\n473: \n474:   /*\n475:    * Response format\n476:    *\n477:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n478:    *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\n479:    *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n480:    * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\n481:    *\n482:    * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. (%d)\"\n508:           \", request rejected or failed.\",\n509:           socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n510:           (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n511:           (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n512:     return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\n513:   case 92:\n514:     failf(data,\n515:           \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. Replies\". /* expect two bytes */\n643:     sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\n644:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n645:   case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n646:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n647:                                \"initial SOCKS5 response\");\n648:     if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n649:       return presult;\n650:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n651:       /* remain in reading state */\n652:       return CURLPX_OK;\n653:     }\n654:     else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\n655:       failf(data, \"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\");\n656:       return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n657:     }\n658:     else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\n659:       /* DONE! failf(data, \"Unable to negotiate SOCKS5 GSS-API context.\");\n674:         return CURLPX_GSSAPI;\n675:       }\n676:     }\n677: #endif\n678:     else {\n679:       /* error */\n680: len += proxy_password_len;\n744:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_SEND);\n745:     sx->outstanding = len;\n746:     sx->outp = socksreq;\n747:   }\n748:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n749:   case presult)\n753:       return presult;\n754:     else if(sx->outstanding) {\n755:       /* remain in sending state */\n756:       return CURLPX_OK;\n757:     }\n758:     sx->outp = socksreq;\n759:     sx->outstanding = 2;\n760:     sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_READ);\n761:     /* FALLTHROUGH */\n762:   case CONNECT_AUTH_READ:\n763:     presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data,     /* remain in reading state */\n769:       return CURLPX_OK;\n770:     }\n771:     /* ignore the first (VER) byte */\n772:     else if(socksreq[1]) { /* status */\n773:       failf(data, \"User was enum resolve_t rc = Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port,\n785:                                       TRUE, &dns);\n786: \n787:       if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n788:         return Summary\n\nThis analysis examines whether the `do_SOCKS5()` function in curl's SOCKS5 proxy handler is reachable from external HTTP/HTTPS input during normal proxy operation.\n\n**Conclusion: REACHABLE from external attacker-controlled input (proxy server responses and user-controlled hostname/port parameters)**\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function is directly reachable when a user configures curl with a SOCKS5 proxy. External attacker-controlled data can reach this function through:\n1. **Proxy server responses** - The function processes data received from the SOCKS5 proxy server\n2. **User-specified hostname/port** - Configuration parameters flow through to this function\n\n---\n\n## 2. Affected Code\n\n**Function:** `do_SOCKS5()`\n**Location:** `lib/socks.c:548-1054`\n**File:** `lib/socks.c`\n\n### Function Purpose\nImplements the SOCKS5 proxy protocol handshake as defined in RFC 1928. This function:\n- Initiates SOCKS5 connection to proxy server\n- Handles authentication (username/password, GSS-API)\n- Sends connection request to remote host through proxy\n- Processes and validates all proxy responses\n- Performs state machine transitions through SOCKS5 protocol phases\n\n---\n\n## 3. Attack Path\n\n### Complete Call Chain (HTTP/HTTPS Entry Point)\n\n```\nmain()\n  └─> curl_easy_perform()\n      └─> multi_perform()\n          └─> curl_multi_perform()\n              └─> multi_socket()\n                  └─> multi_socket_action()\n                      └─> Curl_http_connect() [lib/http.c:1565]\n                          └─> Curl_conn_connect() [lib/cfilters.c:333]\n                              └─> cf->cft->do_connect(cf, data, blocking, done)\n                                  └─> (connection filter chain)\n                                      └─> cf_setup_h1_proxy() [lib/connect.c:1200+]\n                                          └─> Curl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after() [lib/socks.c:1240]\n                                              └─> socks_proxy_cf_connect() [lib/socks.c:1103]\n                                                  └─> connect_SOCKS() [lib/socks.c:1056]\n                                                      └─> do_SOCKS5() [lib/socks.c:548]\n```\n\n### Key Intermediate Functions\n\n| Function | Location | Role |\n|----------|----------|------|\n| `Curl_http_connect()` | lib/http.c:1565 | HTTP protocol handler entry point |\n| `Curl_conn_connect()` | lib/cfilters.c:333 | Connection filter dispatcher |\n| `cf_setup_h1_proxy()` | lib/connect.c:1174+ | Inserts proxy filters into connection chain |\n| `Curl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after()` | lib/socks.c:1240 | SOCKS filter factory function |\n| `socks_proxy_cf_connect()` | lib/socks.c:1103 | SOCKS filter connection handler |\n| `connect_SOCKS()` | lib/socks.c:1056 | Proxy type dispatcher (calls do_SOCKS5 or do_SOCKS4) |\n| `do_SOCKS5()` | lib/socks.c:548 | SOCKS5 protocol implementation |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Severity Assessment\n\n### Reachability Analysis\n\n**YES - REACHABLE from external input**\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function is reachable through the normal user-initiated connection flow when a SOCKS5 proxy is configured.\n\n### Attack Vector & Trigger Conditions\n\n**Attack Vector 1: Direct Proxy Server Response Processing (HIGH IMPACT)**\n- **Requirement:** User specifies `curl https://example.com --proxy socks5://attacker-proxy:1080`\n- **Attacker Control:** Malicious SOCKS5 server (attacker controls proxy endpoint)\n- **Data Flow:**\n  1. User provides proxy URL: `socks5://attacker-proxy:1080`\n  2. Curl connects to proxy server at `attacker-proxy`\n  3. `do_SOCKS5()` processes responses from proxy server\n  4. Attacker sends crafted SOCKS5 protocol responses\n- **Vulnerable Code Paths:**\n  - Line 646-653: Initial SOCKS5 response parsing\n  - Line 960-986: Connect request ACK response parsing\n  - Line 1005-1020: Bind address response parsing\n  - Lines 1004-1020: Address type parsing with variable-length fields\n\n**Attack Vector 2: Hostname Length Handling (MEDIUM IMPACT)**\n- **Requirement:** User specifies `curl https://[hostname] --proxy socks5h://proxy:1080`\n- **Data Flow:**\n  1. User provides target hostname\n  2. Hostname flows through proxy configuration → `sx->hostname`\n  3. Hostname length calculated: `hostname_len = strlen(sx->hostname)` (line 575)\n  4. Hostname used in packet construction at line 906\n- **Potential Issue:** Line 906 casts `hostname_len` (size_t) to `(char)` but line 589 enforces RFC 1928 limit\n- **Mitigating Factor:** Explicit check at line 589 forces local resolution if hostname > 255 characters\n\n**Attack Vector 3: Authentication Credential Processing (MEDIUM IMPACT)**\n- **Requirement:** User provides proxy credentials: `curl --proxy-user user:pass --proxy socks5://proxy:1080`\n- **Data Flow:**\n  1. User provides credentials\n  2. Credentials stored in `sx->proxy_user` and `sx->proxy_password` (line 703-743)\n  3. User/password length validation at lines 727-729, 737-739\n  4. Credentials sent to proxy in SOCKS5 subnegotiation packet\n\n### External Input Reaching do_SOCKS5()\n\n**Data Sources:**\n\n1. **Proxy Server Network Responses** (Primary attack surface):\n   - Initial server response (lines 645-657)\n   - Authentication response (lines 762-776)\n   - Connect request ACK (lines 951-986)\n   - Bind address field (lines 1005-1020)\n   - Address type field (socksreq[3], line 1005)\n   - Address length field (socksreq[4], line 1007)\n\n2. **User-Controlled Configuration** (Secondary attack surface):\n   - Hostname parameter (from `curl https://hostname`)\n   - Proxy server address (from `--proxy` flag)\n   - Proxy credentials (from `--proxy-user` flag)\n   - Port number (from target URL or `--proxy` flag)\n\n3. **Command-Line Input**:\n   - User can control hostname length\n   - User can specify any SOCKS5 proxy endpoint\n   - User can provide malformed proxy URLs\n\n---\n\n## 5. Remediation & Security Considerations\n\n### Existing Protections Found\n\n1. **RFC 1928 Hostname Length Check (Line 589)**\n   ```c\n   if(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n     socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n   }\n   ```\n   **Effect:** Enforces RFC 1928 requirement that domain names in SOCKS5 packets cannot exceed 255 bytes\n\n2. **Authentication Credential Length Validation (Lines 727-729, 737-739)**\n   ```c\n   if(proxy_user_len > 255) {\n     failf(data, \"Excessive user name length for proxy auth\");\n     return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n   }\n   ```\n   **Effect:** Prevents username/password from exceeding SOCKS5 protocol limits\n\n3. **Protocol Version Validation (Lines 654-657)**\n   ```c\n   else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\n     failf(data, \"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\");\n     return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n   }\n   ```\n   **Effect:** Validates proxy response format\n\n4. **Buffer Limits**\n   - Line 287: `DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600)` ensures adequate buffer space\n   - Hostname maximum of 255 characters enforced by RFC 1928 check\n\n### Potential Vulnerability Areas\n\n1. **Variable-Length Field Parsing (Lines 1005-1020)**\n   - Code calculates packet size based on `socksreq[3]` (address type) and `socksreq[4]` (length)\n   - If proxy sends malformed address type or length values, parsing could be incorrect\n   - However, bounds checking exists (lines 1014-1020)\n\n2. **DNS Response Buffer (Line 822)**\n   ```c\n   char dest[MAX_IPADR_LEN] = \"unknown\";\n   ```\n   - Used for printable address formatting only (line 832)\n   - Not a security concern\n\n### Recommended Mitigation Strategies\n\n**For Protocol Robustness:**\n\n1. **Enhance Bind Address Validation**\n   ```c\n   // After calculating len from address type:\n   if(len < 10 || len > data->set.buffer_size - 10) {\n     failf(data, \"Invalid SOCKS5 response packet size\");\n     return CURLPX_BAD_ADDRESS_TYPE;\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Validate Address Type Field**\n   ```c\n   // Line 1005:\n   if(socksreq[3] < 1 || socksreq[3] > 4) {\n     failf(data, \"SOCKS5 invalid address type: %d\", socksreq[3]);\n     return CURLPX_BAD_ADDRESS_TYPE;\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Add Hostname Sanitization**\n   - Already done well at line 589, maintain this check\n   - Consider log warning for large hostnames\n\n4. **Proxy Server Trust Verification**\n   - Current code trusts proxy responses implicitly\n   - Consider adding optional proxy certificate pinning for future enhancement\n   - Add timeout protection for proxy responses\n\n**For Attack Surface Reduction:**\n\n1. **User Warning for Untrusted Proxies**\n   - Display warning when connecting to proxy without HTTPS encryption\n   - Suggest using HTTPS proxy URL when available\n\n2. **Input Validation at Entry**\n   - Hostname validation at proxy configuration time (not just at protocol level)\n   - Pre-flight checks for obviously malformed targets\n\n---\n\n## 6. Conclusion\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function is **REACHABLE from external attacker-controlled input** in the following scenarios:\n\n1. **Malicious SOCKS5 Proxy Server** - An attacker who controls or intercepts the SOCKS5 proxy endpoint can send crafted protocol responses to trigger vulnerability code paths in `do_SOCKS5()`\n\n2. **Legitimate Use with Untrusted Proxy** - A user connecting through an HTTP/HTTPS request through a public or untrusted SOCKS5 proxy is exposing their curl client to the proxy's control\n\n3. **User-Supplied Hostname Attacks** - While protections exist, hostname parameters flow directly into `do_SOCKS5()` and are processed by the protocol handler\n\n### Security Posture\n\n- **Current Status:** Well-protected against common buffer overflow vectors\n- **RFC 1928 Compliance:** Good (enforces 255-byte hostname limit)\n- **Input Validation:** Adequate for protocol requirements\n- **Recommended:** Add enhanced packet size validation and address type validation for defense-in-depth\n\nThe function is appropriate for its intended use case but users should be cautious about SOCKS5 proxy sources, as the proxy server has significant control over the protocol exchange.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2179,"cache_read_input_tokens":69477,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2179},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7c2844fd-937a-4b9d-b22d-370f30126a68","uuid":"41c6705c-0a67-405c-a74c-70693ede6cd9"}
